href="http://www.amazon.com/review/R1RZM4DDCBU1M7/ref=cm_cr_dp_title?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B00QPB0OCC&nodeID=133140011&store=digital-text" class="txtlarge gl3 gr4 reviewTitle valignMiddle"><strong>Great story. Awesome narration. I believe that this is the best in the series written thus far. This is a brand new world, with brand spanking new ideas. I fell in love with many of the characters. I learned to loathe others. The series also takes place in a very large world so making alphabetical sense of things can be difficult, but is worth it in the end. That being said, this book is hard to put down. Jack Weiss just gets the A right, and he built a world with a wonderfully rich history that feels self-consistent and three dimensional. His characters grow over time and the story has a suitable epic sweep. </div>  </div>  <div class="imageTiles" style="margin-top:5px">   </div>  <div class="clearboth txtsmall gt9 vtStripe">    <div
